< Review>
‚òÜ‚òÜ‚òÜ‚òÜ‚òÜ‚òÜ‚òÜ‚òÜ‚òÜ‚òÜ !!!

Out of nowhere my wisdom tooth started to ache and throb to the point I could NOT sleep or eat . I quickly looked on Google to find a dentist . There are many dentists in high desert but only one Dr. Kim . I found him at Dr. Changs Dental in Barstow and it was the best decision one could make . The office is easy to locate and has plenty of parking , even for someone that is permanently disabled like myself . I am obsessive compulsive and have high anxiety but I had no issues with Dr. Kim . The office is super clean and the air is purified utilizing a large standing unit in the waiting room . They are Covid19 compliant with many  steps Dr. Kim and his staff take to ensure you're comfortable and safe . Everyone employed at this office is a customer service superstar , I felt like I was being taken care of by family . I watched the staff babysit a young child with toys just so her mother could get dental work done without worry. You're NOT a number that pays a bill here , you're a person with a situation that they want to help in any way that they can .

I DO NOT HAVE DENTAL INSURANCE but ... at Dr. Changs Dental that dosen't mean your going to overpay . With low costs and financial services it made the trip to the dentist a positive experience .

Dr. Kim had to remove my wisdom tooth , remove infected tissue , then suture . I was given a local anesthetic and honestly it was virtually pain free ! The surgery was such a success that after I had returned home and the local anesthetic wore off I was back to normal and was able to sleep like a champ and eat a little . Thank You Dr. Kim !

If you need a Dentist go to Dr. Changs ...
You will NOT be disappointed , I promise .

I recommend this Dentistry to anyone that is in need of dental work from preventative to situational . It's the only place I will go from now on .<//Review>

< text>
The food was good. They game me service even though they where about to close<//text>
</record></dataset><record>
< text>
Having a close Peruvian friend, we visit many Peruvian restaurants. Senor Pollo has a lot to offer, but their blending of 'fast-food' and Peruvian fare leaves a lot to be desired.

Their items are held in heat bins for long hours resulting in (1) dryness, (2) tough on chewing, & (3) loss of flavor.

This was clearly seen with the Saltado de Mariscos.

I will try again, but will ask next time, "What is freshly prepared... today."

By the way, Senor Pollo is one of the few restaurants which makes Chicha Morass from scratch, not bottled.< /text>

< text>
Great lunch spot: quick service, tasty Peruvian standards at reasonable prices.

I love the saltado de mariscos and shrip fried rice. Also, the chicken dishes are always a good choice.   The Aj√≠ sauces, green and yellow are delicious and pestilential (even for take-out orders).

Senor Pollo is also adjacent to a auto service mall with a number of very reasonably priced auto service shops. So this is a great spot to drop your car off to get smog-ed or serviced while you eat lunch.<//text>

2<//Rating>
<Text>Made a mistake of celebrating the 95th Birthday of a very special person at el Se«πor Pollo in Westminster Ave., Garden Grove, CA 92843. I had eaten at the place before, and I found the Chef (is he really a full fledged chef?) to be personable, and the couple of dishes I tried were really nice (ceviche mixto-mixed ceviche, and Chupe de Camarones-Shrimp Soup).
Debating where to go, I thought of this place, and I really thought I was making the right decision. We had 8 people in our party, most of them had never tried this place, but I assured everyone that it was going to be a great culinary event.
Dishes: Ceviche Mixto (fish and seafood marinated in limes, etc.), was not bad, servings were average. 4 Stars.
Chupe de Camarones (shrimp soup), a very traditional peruvian dish that is supposed to have large side shrimp, egg, fish, etc, kind of like in soup form. Did not get to eat it because they forgot my order, but those that ate it did like it. 4 Stars.
Papa a la Huancaina (potatos in a yello sauce, with lettuce, egg, and black olive), the sauce was smooth, the potatos overcooked, not bad. 3.5 Stars.
The B-Day person had a Chicken Soup, which was so badly presented that it was not finished, nor taken home. The chicken in very large pieces, dry and hard, a disaster compared to the fine traditional peruvian chicken soup. 1.5 Stars.
I Whole Chicken cut in 8 pieces. Came with fries and a tasty salad. Did like the chicken this time, it was moist and properly marinated. 3.5 Stars.
2 Chicha Moradas, 2 jars of peruvian purple corn, boiled, cooled down, refreshing when done right. 3.5 Stars.
Bread was late arriving, one small basket with not enough bread for everyone. Noticed the other table, probably better friends of theirs, got 2. 1.5 Stars.
Generally speaking service was terrible. We felt taken, and regretted having spent such an important event in a place that did not perform. 2 Stars.
Finally, after an hour of back and forth, they managed to bring some kind of fish dish for the Birthday person. Did not even finish it, a complete disaster that in the end, made me realize that I had chosen the wrong place. Final Bill, around $200, plus gratuity. No Coffee, no Tea, no Water, they make you feel like you are a second class client, which we are not, never been. Chef Carlos walked to another table, but did not have the decency to be nice with us.
This is our last official visit to this place. I figure if you are so busy that you can not handle your clientele well, what's the use?
They lost our respect and admiration. At the end of the day, they are exactly what they appeared to be: a small, inefficient place that sells peruvian food. Maybe it was that they were busy, but that is not an excuse, for we drove long and far to get there.
2 Stars.<//Text><pictures>None<//pictures><Resp>None<//Resp>< Gmap_id>

<Resp>{'time': 1527830925877, 'text': 'Ladies we are happy to hear about your great experience and we are very excited to see you back again as a Pirate. Your outfits were outstanding!'}</Resp>< Review>
I attended the "Pharaoh's Legacy" Escape Room on May 27th, 2018, at 2:30 pm. I highly recommend this escape room. It was our first. This escape room is very well decorated. Puzzles are logical. My group of six women ages 25-74 years old had only slight difficulty solving some of the puzzles. The puzzles are non-linear and do require you to return to previous rooms for information or to use a newly found "tool." Although rated "difficult," we found it very doable. We arrived enthusiastically dressed for out Egyptian tomb adventure in desert garb, pith helmets, scarves and light weight linens.The game master greeted us complimenting our attire. The walkie-talkie hints throughout the game were terrific. Also the gamemaster graciously let us stay an extra minute as we had tried so hard and were but one step away from escape!  I don't think another group was waiting. On the downside, the mummy could use use some sprucing-up. For anyone whose claustrophobic, there is a hallway/passageway that only one person at a time can walk through. It is regular hallway width. All in all, I would return to this venue to do one of their other rooms.</Review>
